○007920○Back when I'd only just arrived in this world, Yuri had told me the Battlefront's objective in this very place.
●007920●刚刚来到这个世界不久的时候，由理在这个地方告诉了我战线的目的。

○007921○Back then, I hadn't been interested at all.
●007921●那个时候并没有兴趣。

○007922○All I could think about was staying safe until my memories came back to me.
●007922●只是想『安全』地度过取回记忆之前的这段『时间』。

○007923○But somewhere along the way, I realized that the time I'd spent with them had built up strong bonds between us.
●007923●但是我发现了，和这些人一起度过的『时间』，已经结成了深深的牵绊。

○007924○From here on, this world will carry on for years, for decades.
●007924●从现在开始，这个世界还会持续数年，持续几十年。

○007925○A world where only time is infinite.
●007925●只有时间是无限的世界。

○007926○A Battlefront, rebelling against God.
●007926●反抗神的战线。

○007927○...And, now that I've recovered my memories, I've truly joined their ranks.
●007927●…在取回了记忆的现在，我重新成为了其中的一员。

○007928○All of it for Yuri's sake alone.
●007928●全部都是为了由理。

○007929○I'll keep on fighting in this world.
●007929●我会在这个世界上继续战斗。

○007930○For my own sake, and Yuri's as well.
●007930●为了我自己，也为了由理。

○007931○I'll keep on fighting in this world.
●007931●我会在这个世界上继续战斗。

○007932○I'll give it everything I have, all for Hinata's sake.
●007932●我会为了日向，献出自己的全部。

○007933○I'll keep on fighting alongside Hinata in this world.
●007933●在这个世界上，和日向一起继续战斗。
